R Assignment 1

Chapter 4 Questions

4.1 Q1

List all variables in the data set cdc.R. For each variable, determine if it is Categorical, or numerical, and if numerical, if it is discrete or continuous.

names(cdc)
## [1] "genhlth"  "exerany"  "hlthplan" "smoke100" "height"   "weight"   "wtdesire"
## [8] "age"      "gender"

  • Gen health: Categorical

  • Exerany: categorical

  • Hlthplan; Categorical

  • Smoke: Categorical

  • Height: Numerical: continuous

  • Weight” Numerical: Continuous

  • WtDesired: Numerical Continous

  • Age: Numerical Discrete

  • Gender: Categorical

4.2 Q3

How many people were used in this survey?

20,000
